Except for the hotel staff, outsiders are not allowed to enter the guest area. The privacy is very strong, which makes me feel very safe and assured. I want to give this hotel a big thumbs up. The hotel is in Jimei Academy Village, close to Jiageng Park, about a five-minute walk away. It is also very convenient to go to Aoyuan. There is also the nearby Shigu Road Food Street, which has many local snacks in Xiamen. I also ate earthworm jelly, which is very fresh and delicious. The hotel also has a complete range of dining options. There is a seafood buffet on the first floor, a Hong Kong-style refreshment in the Fujian and Guangdong Pavilion, and a Vbar Seaview Restaurant on the fifth floor of Area B. The chef is too cold, and the food is rich and varied, fresh and delicious. There is also a constant temperature indoor swimming pool and an outdoor children's playground in the hotel park, where you can climb, slide and play on the trampoline, which is very safe and tidy. Another place my children like very much is the hot spring water park, which is the most popular place in summer. Here you can completely free your hands.
